 \"text\": \"The CSS style change propagation through Chromium's Blink rendering engine follows a clear pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Style Resolution** (StyleResolver): Located in `third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/style_resolver.h`, the `StyleResolver` class is responsible for resolving computed styles for DOM elements. It maintains a 1-1 relationship with Document and uses methods like `ResolveStyle()` to compute the final styles based on CSS rules, cascade, and inheritance.\\n\\n2. **Layout Tree** (LayoutObject): The base class `LayoutObject` in `third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/layout_object.h` represents the layout tree structure. Each DOM element with a corresponding LayoutObject is laid out based on its computed style. LayoutObject inherits from both GarbageCollected and DisplayItemClient, establishing the connection to the painting system.\\n\\n3. **Paint Layers** (PaintLayer): The `PaintLayer` class in `third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/paint_layer.h` represents layers in the paint tree. PaintLayer objects are created for elements that require special rendering properties (positioning, transforms, filters, etc.). Each PaintLayer manages its layout object and controls the painting operations for that layer.\\n\\n4. **Paint Controller** (PaintController): Defined in `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h`, the `PaintController` class orchestrates the painting process. It manages display items, handles caching, and records paint operations. The PaintController maintains the current paint chunk properties and controls the serialization of display items.\\n\\n5. **Display List** (DisplayItemList): The `DisplayItemList` class in `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/display_item_list.h` is a container for display items of various types.
